styling="[object Object]" weight="[object Object]">With whom does RS share my information?</h4><p class="styled-text-component-module_styled-text-component__1Pric styled-text-component-module_text-size-paragraph__2PEy7 styled-text-component-module_black__FQNIL styled-text-component-module_mobile-black__6JO72" decoration="[object Object]" padding="[object style="--desktop-padding-top:0px;--desktop-padding-right:0px;--desktop-padding-bottom:16px;--desktop-padding-left:0px;--mobile-padding-top:0px;--mobile-padding-right:0px;--mobile-padding-bottom:8px;--mobile-padding-left:0px;--desktop-text-align:left;--mobile-text-align:left;text-decoration:;font-style:normal" styling="[object Object]" weight="[object Object]">The company named on this site is a distributor of RS for your country, and RS operates this site on behalf of that distributor. Therefore all personal information collected by this site which is necessary for the distributor to fulfil your order will be passed to the distributor, and all other personal information collected by this site may be passed to the distributor. Any other sharing of information by RS's distributor will be notified to you by the distributor in accordance with local law.</p><p class="styled-text-component-module_styled-text-component__1Pric styled-text-component-module_text-size-paragraph__2PEy7 styled-text-component-module_black__FQNIL styled-text-component-module_mobile-black__6JO72" decoration="[object Object]" padding="[object Object]" style="--desktop-padding-top:0px;--desktop-padding-right:0px;--desktop-padding-bottom:16px;--desktop-padding-left:0px;--mobile-padding-top:0px;--mobile-padding-right:0px;--mobile-padding-bottom:8px;--mobile-padding-left:0px;--desktop-text-align:left;--mobile-text-align:left;text-decoration:;font-style:normal" styling="[object Object]" weight="[object Object]">In the event that RS's distributor for your country changes, your personal information may be disclosed to the new distributor.</p><p class="styled-text-component-module_styled-text-component__1Pric styled-text-component-module_text-size-paragraph__2PEy7 styled-text-component-module_black__FQNIL styled-text-component-module_mobile-black__6JO72" decoration="[object Object]" padding="[object Object]" style="--desktop-padding-top:0px;--desktop-padding-right:0px;--desktop-padding-bottom:16px;--desktop-padding-left:0px;--mobile-padding-top:0px;--mobile-padding-right:0px;--mobile-padding-bottom:8px;--mobile-padding-left:0px;--desktop-text-align:left;--mobile-text-align:left;text-decoration:;font-style:normal" styling="[object Object]" weight="[object Object]">RS may need to disclose your information to organisations working on our behalf anywhere in the world, but will never sell, rent, or give away information that personally identifies customers to third parties. From time to time, we may release aggregated and anonymised marketing statistics to business partners, or may use these in press releases, advertising, or published reports. RS is a member of a world-wide group of companies of which Electrocomponents plc is the parent company - RS may share aggregated and anonymised marketing statistics with this group of companies. RS may also disclose user information in special cases when we believe that disclosing this information is necessary to identify, contact or bring legal action against someone who may be causing injury to or interference with RS's rights or property, other RS Online users, or anyone else that could be harmed by such activities. In addition, RS may disclose user information when the law requires it. </p></div></div></div></div><div class="campaign-page-component_campaign-content-container__2q4q4 inner-page-wrapper styling="[object Object]" weight="[object Object]">The following information is gathered when you register: Username, Password, Security Password, your name, telephone number, fax number, email address, company name, address, company's area of business, job technology, job function, purchasing influence, number of employees in your company, your primary product interest and how you heard about the site. We may also record some details of how you use the site, such as adverts you click on or products you search for.</p><p class="styled-text-component-module_styled-text-component__1Pric styled-text-component-module_text-size-paragraph__2PEy7 styled-text-component-module_black__FQNIL styled-text-component-module_mobile-black__6JO72" decoration="[object Object]" padding="[object Object]" style="--desktop-padding-top:0px;--desktop-padding-right:0px;--desktop-padding-bottom:16px;--desktop-padding-left:0px;--mobile-padding-top:0px;--mobile-padding-right:0px;--mobile-padding-bottom:8px;--mobile-padding-left:0px;--desktop-text-align:left;--mobile-text-align:left;text-decoration:;font-style:normal" styling="[object Object]" weight="[object Object]">In addition, we keep copies of information you submit when you send email feedback to the site, ask a technical question, or report a problem. styling="[object Object]" weight="[object Object]">What does RS do to protect your personal data online?</h4><p class="styled-text-component-module_styled-text-component__1Pric styling="[object Object]" weight="[object Object]">In order to ensure the security and protection of your personal details whenever you submit any sensitive information such as credit card number and account details, we use 128 bit Secure Sockets Layer (SSL) encryption - the latest technology to encode and protect your data - which is your guarantee for a safe and secure transaction. The RS VeriSign Security Guarantee pops up whenever you submit sensitive information as an indication that the current information will be encrypted. This means that your information is protected and safe to submit.</p><p class="styled-text-component-module_styled-text-component__1Pric styled-text-component-module_text-size-paragraph__2PEy7 styled-text-component-module_black__FQNIL styled-text-component-module_mobile-black__6JO72" decoration="[object Object]" padding="[object Object]" style="--desktop-padding-top:0px;--desktop-padding-right:0px;--desktop-padding-bottom:16px;--desktop-padding-left:0px;--mobile-padding-top:0px;--mobile-padding-right:0px;--mobile-padding-bottom:8px;--mobile-padding-left:0px;--desktop-text-align:left;--mobile-text-align:left;text-decoration:;font-style:normal" styling="[object Object]" weight="[object Object]">Sensitive credit card information stored on our in-house systems is also held in encrypted format.</p><p class="styled-text-component-module_styled-text-component__1Pric styled-text-component-module_text-size-paragraph__2PEy7 styled-text-component-module_black__FQNIL styled-text-component-module_mobile-black__6JO72" decoration="[object Object]" padding="[object Object]" style="--desktop-padding-top:0px;--desktop-padding-right:0px;--desktop-padding-bottom:16px;--desktop-padding-left:0px;--mobile-padding-top:0px;--mobile-padding-right:0px;--mobile-padding-bottom:8px;--mobile-padding-left:0px;--desktop-text-align:left;--mobile-text-align:left;text-decoration:;font-style:normal" styling="[object Object]" weight="[object Object]">Note: If you rely upon the graphical indication on your browser screen (such as the padlock icon in Internet Explorer) this may not always indicate that a secure communication is taking place. styling="[object Object]" weight="[object Object]">Your RS Online Account Information and RS Online Personal Profile are password-protected so that you and only you have access to this personal information. We recommend that you do not divulge your password to anyone. RS Online will never ask you for your password in an unsolicited phone call or in an unsolicited email. Also remember to close your browser window when you have finished your work. This is to ensure that others cannot access your personal or business information if you share a computer or are using a computer in a public place. </p></div></div></div></div><div Any other use by RS's distributor will be notified to you by the distributor in accordance with local law.</p><p class="styled-text-component-module_styled-text-component__1Pric styled-text-component-module_text-size-paragraph__2PEy7 styled-text-component-module_black__FQNIL styled-text-component-module_mobile-black__6JO72" decoration="[object Object]" padding="[object Object]" style="--desktop-padding-top:0px;--desktop-padding-right:0px;--desktop-padding-bottom:16px;--desktop-padding-left:0px;--mobile-padding-top:0px;--mobile-padding-right:0px;--mobile-padding-bottom:8px;--mobile-padding-left:0px;--desktop-text-align:left;--mobile-text-align:left;text-decoration:;font-style:normal" styling="[object Object]" weight="[object Object]">RS collects your personal information to provide you with customised and relevant information on your home page when you visit the site. RS also does research on our users' demographics, interests, and behaviour based on the information provided to us through registration, from our server log files or from surveys.
